<name>Candace Carteen<//name><pictures>None< /pictures>< Review>
Very strange McDonalds. It is attached to a gas station where you can enter through the gas station door or the McDonald's door and end up in the same space. It's not one of those places that has a very good parking lot. In fact when I first came here I actually thought it was a drive through because I didn't see any parking spaces for McDonald's patrons to park. Just before heading out, I finally found approximately 10 spaces tuck into the far corner by the drive-thru that didn't appear to belong to the gas station. Because of their they are pretty difficult to get into, and almost impossible to get out of.
The entire place is really not that clean. I have been here almost an hour and in that time no one has cleaned any of the tables or cleaned the garbage off of the floors.
They do have a pretty steady clientele mostly the drive-thru but many that walk in. Their menu seems complete. Prices are about the same across the board as other McDonald's I have visited. Yes, they do have high chairs!
The personnel seemed extremely pleasant. They tend to talk to each other well, get the job done and in a reasonable time. This is truly a fast food restaurant, the wait here is very short.
If you're looking for quiet, this is not the place to come. There's a lot of noise that comes from the gas station part of the building, the road that runs right beside the building, the drive-through and just the traffic of McDonald's workers and patrons themself.
Would I come back here? Actually I would. There's nothing here that scares me off. I feel safe, I feel secure, and the food was McDonald's food. Isn't that what I walked in for?
If you enjoyed my review, please LIKE below and, as always, have an amazing day!</Review>

<Review>I work across the street from this McDondals location, so it is USALLY
convenient. But not today. There is a gas station at this location as well, so
on my lunch break I thought I'd knock out lunch and getting gas at the same
time. So I got my gas and then proceeded to the drive-thru line. Usually it is
very quick, but it was way slow today. There were 3 or 4 cars in front of me and
i waited over 10 mins, and still wasn't at the mic to order. Thats when a car
from off the street came and cut me in line. Now I know it's not your fault that
the customer was rude, but when it's that busy, there is usually an employee
standing by the drive-thru helping take orders and directing the line. If they
were out there, then it wouldn't have caused such a problem. They could even
close that second entry from the street during busy hours to avoid this.Also, I
called this McDonalds location to let the manager know what was going on, and
